Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-07-29 Fedora Release Engineering - 2.7.1-134 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_33_Mass_Rebuild
2020-07-27 VÃ­t Ondruch - 2.7.1-133 - Disable LTO, which appear to cause issues with SIGSEV handler. - Avoid possible timeout errors in TestBugReporter#test_bug_reporter_add.
2020-06-24 Jun Aruga - 2.7.1-132 - Add ruby-default-gems dependency on irb. Resolves: rhbz#1850541
2020-06-24 VÃ­t Ondruch - 2.7.1-132 - Fix `require` behavior allowing to load libraries multiple times. Resolves: rhbz#1835836
2020-05-15 VÃ­t Ondruch - 2.7.1-131 - Relax rubygems-devel dependency on rubygems.
2020-04-08 VÃ­t Ondruch - 2.7.1-130 - Bundle did_you_mean into StdLib. Resolves: rhbz#1817178 - Prevent issues with openssl loading when RubyGems are disabled.
2020-04-02 VÃ­t Ondruch - 2.7.1-129 - Add ruby-default-gems subpackage shipping all extra default gem content. - Bundle Racc into StdLib.
2020-04-01 VÃ­t Ondruch - 2.7.1-128 - Upgrade to Ruby 2.7.1. - Fix FTBFS due to glibc 2.31.9000 implementing lchmod(2).
2020-01-28 VÃ­t Ondruch - 2.7.0-127 - Provide StdLib links for Racc and install it by default.
2020-01-16 VÃ­t Ondruch - 2.7.0-126 - Make rubygem(did_you_mean) hard dependency.
